What Exactly Triggers Error 8133\n\nError 8133 is **not stored in a database or SharedPreferences**. This is precisely what `pm disable-user --user 0 com.samsung.android.kgclient` does.\n\nSource: `/services/sources/com/samsung/android/knoxguard/service/utils/IntegritySeUtil.java` in [488315/samsung_framework](https://github.com/488315/samsung_framework) on GitHub.\n\n## 2. How `handleBootCompleted()` Decides to Trigger 8133\n\nThe exact flow in `SystemIntentProcessor.handleBootCompleted()`:\n\n1. Calls `Utils.getStateAndSetToKGSystemProperty()` -- reads TA state from RPMB via `KnoxGuardNative.tz_getTAState(0)`, maps it to system property `knox.kg.state`\n2. Checks `IntegritySeUtil.checkTaIntegrity()` -- validates TA error codes (513, 519, -1006). If failed, locks with TA error.\n3. Checks `IntegritySeUtil.checkAPSerialIntegrity()` -- validates AP serial from TZ is 32-char hex. If failed, locks with error 1002.\n4. Calls `IntegritySeUtil.checkKGClientIntegrityAndEnableComponentsWithFlag(context, state, true)` -- **this is where 8133 is generated**. It checks:\n   - **Signature**: `PackageManager.checkSignatures(\"android\", \"com.samsung.android.kgclient\")` -- must match platform\n   - **isEnabled**: `getApplicationInfo(\"com.samsung.android.kgclient\").enabled` -- **must be true**\n   - **isValidVersion**: `versionCode >= 300000000`\n   - **6 components enabled**: KGDeviceAdminReceiver, SystemIntentReceiver, SelfupdateReceiver, KGEventService, AlarmService, KGProvider\n5. If integrity check returns `isOk = false`, it calls `Utils.lockSeDevice(context, String.valueOf(toErrorCode(result)))` -- this produces error 8133.\n6. **The third parameter `true`** means \"try to re-enable components if in maintenance mode.\" On normal boot, it just checks.\n\n**Critical insight**: The check happens EVERY boot. There is no stored \"tampering flag.\" The error is dynamically computed based on the current state of kgclient. If kgclient is re-enabled with all components enabled, the check will pass and 8133 will NOT appear.\n\nSource: `SystemIntentProcessor.java` in the same repo.\n\n## 3. Is There a Specific File/DB/SharedPreference Recording Tampering?\n\n**No.** The 8133 error is NOT stored anywhere persistent. It is computed fresh each boot by checking:\n- `PackageManager.getApplicationInfo(\"com.samsung.android.kgclient\", 0).enabled` -- app enabled state\n- `PackageManager.getPackageInfo(\"com.samsung.android.kgclient\", 14)` -- component enabled state (flag 14 = GET_RECEIVERS|GET_SERVICES|GET_PROVIDERS)\n\nThese states ARE persistent though -- they're stored in `/data/system/packages.xml` (the `<package>` entry for kgclient) and in per-user package restrictions at `/data/system/users/0/package-restrictions.xml`. When you ran `pm disable-user --user 0`, it wrote a `<pkg name=\"com.samsung.android.kgclient\" enabled=\"2\">` (disabled) entry.\n\n**Re-enabling kgclient should fix this**, because the check will find the app enabled and components enabled.
